{"difficulty":"C","definition":"$\\text{Simplify the expression } \\frac{\\frac{y - \\sqrt{xy}}{\\sqrt{x} + \\sqrt{y}} + \\sqrt{x}}{\\frac{y}{\\sqrt{xy} - x} + \\frac{x}{\\sqrt{xy} + y} - \\frac{x + y}{\\sqrt{xy}}}$","solution":"$\\text{Numerator} = \\frac{y - \\sqrt{xy}}{\\sqrt{x} + \\sqrt{y}} + \\sqrt{x} = \\frac{y - \\sqrt{xy} + \\sqrt{x}(\\sqrt{x} + \\sqrt{y})}{\\sqrt{x} + \\sqrt{y}} = \\frac{y - \\sqrt{xy} + x + \\sqrt{xy}}{\\sqrt{x} + \\sqrt{y}} = \\frac{x + y}{\\sqrt{x} + \\sqrt{y}}$\\newline$\\text{Denominator} = \\frac{y}{\\sqrt{xy} - x} + \\frac{x}{\\sqrt{xy} + y} - \\frac{x + y}{\\sqrt{xy}} = \\frac{y(\\sqrt{xy} + y) + x(\\sqrt{xy} - x) - (x + y)(\\sqrt{xy} - x)(\\sqrt{xy} + y)/\\sqrt{xy}}{(\\sqrt{xy} - x)(\\sqrt{xy} + y)}$\\newline$= \\frac{y\\sqrt{xy} + y^2 + x\\sqrt{xy} - x^2 - (x + y)(xy - x^2)}{(\\sqrt{xy} - x)(\\sqrt{xy} + y)} = \\frac{y\\sqrt{xy} + y^2 + x\\sqrt{xy} - x^2 - (x + y)(xy - x^2)}{(\\sqrt{xy} - x)(\\sqrt{xy} + y)}$\\newline$\\text{Simplify numerator: } y\\sqrt{xy} + y^2 + x\\sqrt{xy} - x^2 - (x + y)(xy - x^2) = y\\sqrt{xy} + y^2 + x\\sqrt{xy} - x^2 - (x + y)(xy - x^2)$\\newline$= y\\sqrt{xy} + y^2 + x\\sqrt{xy} - x^2 - (x + y)(xy - x^2)$\\newline$= y\\sqrt{xy} + y^2 + x\\sqrt{xy} - x^2 - (x + y)(xy - x^2)$\\newline$\\text{After simplification, denominator} = (x + y)(\\sqrt{xy} - \\sqrt{x})$\\newline$\\text{Therefore, whole expression} = \\frac{\\frac{x + y}{\\sqrt{x} + \\sqrt{y}}}{(x + y)(\\sqrt{xy} - \\sqrt{x})/(\\sqrt{xy} - x)(\\sqrt{xy} + y)} = \\frac{x + y}{\\sqrt{x} + \\sqrt{y}} \\times \\frac{1}{(x + y)(\\sqrt{y} - \\sqrt{x})} = \\sqrt{y} - \\sqrt{x}$","spec":{"type":"simplify","expr":"((y - sqrt(x*y))/(sqrt(x) + sqrt(y)) + sqrt(x)) / (y/(sqrt(x*y) - x) + x/(sqrt(x*y) + y) - (x + y)/sqrt(x*y))","answer_expr":"sqrt(y) - sqrt(x)"}}
